#OnThisDay in 2005, #NewJersey passed its 1st felony state law addressing trafficking in persons. AB 2730 established sex and labor trafficking as first degree felonies. It also allows courts to forfeit any assets used &amp; order restitution to victims. #OTD #EndTrafficking #TVPA20 https://t.co/04eiUUeJaj

The answer to yesterday's #TriviaTuesday is False: Human trafficking is often confused with human smuggling which involves illegal border crossings. In fact the crime of human trafficking does not require any movement. Survivors can be  trafficked in home towns, even their homes. https://t.co/KrHdEADjCT

It's #TriviaTuesday! #TestYourKnowledge during human #traffickingawarenessmonth below and tune in tomorrow for the answer. Statement: Human trafficking involves moving, traveling or transporting a person across state or national borders.
It's #TriviaTuesday! #TestYourKnowledge during human #traffickingawarenessmonth below and tune in tomorrow for the answer. Statement: Human trafficking involves moving, traveling or transporting a person across state or national borders.
